<script>
// news rotation timeout variable to be passed to a rotate function
var news_rotation   = "3000";
$(function(){
$('div[id^=topnewssub_]').each(function(){ this.is_animate = 0; });
$('#top-highlights')[0].counter = 0;
$('#top-highlights')[0].rotate = 1;
$('#top-highlights')[0].selected = $('div[id^=topnewssub_]:first');
$( 'div[id^=topnewsmain_]' )
.mouseover(function(){ $('#top-highlights')[0].rotate = 0; })
.mouseout(function(){ $('#top-highlights')[0].rotate = 1; $( 'div[id^=topnewssub_]' ).removeClass('select') });
__news_rotation_func = function() {
if ( $('#top-highlights')[0].rotate == 1 ) {
var highlights = $('#top-highlights');
var current = highlights[0].counter % 3;
highlights[0].counter++;
var next = highlights[0].counter % 3;
$( '#topnewssub_' + current.toString() ).removeClass('hover').css({ opacity: 1.0 });
$( '#topnewssub_' + next.toString() ).addClass('hover');
$( 'div[id^=topnewsmain_]', highlights  ).hide();
$( '#topnewsmain_' + next.toString(), highlights  ).show();
/*
$( '#topnewssub_' + next.toString() ).css( { opacity: 0.5 });
$( '#topnewssub_' + current.toString() ).animate( { opacity: 0.5 }, 750, function(){
$( '#topnewssub_' + current.toString() ).removeClass('hover').css({ opacity: 1.0 });
$( '#topnewssub_' + next.toString() ).animate( { opacity: 1.0 }, 750 );
});
$( '#topnewsmain_' + current.toString(), highlights  ).fadeOut( 1500 );
highlights[0].selected = $( '#topnewssub_' + next.toString() );
$( '#topnewssub_' + next.toString() ).addClass('hover');
$( '#topnewsmain_' + next.toString(), highlights  ).fadeIn( 1500 );
*/
}
}
$('#top-highlights').get(0).timer = $._timer( 5000, __news_rotation_func );
});
</script>
